[30;1m86 | [0m[35mPyGEOS functions support multithreading. More specifically, the Global[0m
[30;1m87 | [0m[35mInterpreter Lock (GIL) is released during function execution. Normally in Python, the[0m
[30;1m88 | [0m[35mGIL prevents multiple threads from computing at the same time. PyGEOS functions[0m
[30;1m89 | [0m[35minternally releases this constraint so that the heavy lifting done by GEOS can be[0m
[30;1m90 | [0m[35mdone in parallel, from a single Python process.[0m
[30;1m91 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m93 | [0m[35m## Version-String Flavors[0m
[30;1m94 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m95 | [0m[35mCode which uses Versioneer can learn about its version string at runtime by[0m
[30;1m96 | [0m[35mimporting `_version` from your main `__init__.py` file and running the[0m
[30;1m97 | [0m[35m`get_versions()` function. From the "outside" (e.g. in `setup.py`), you can[0m
[30;1m98 | [0m[35mimport the top-level `versioneer.py` and run `get_versions()`.[0m

[30;1m72 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m73 | [0m[35mVersioneer works by adding a special `_version.py` file into your source[0m
[30;1m74 | [0m[35mtree, where your `__init__.py` can import it. This `_version.py` knows how to[0m
[30;1m75 | [0m[35mdynamically ask the VCS tool for version information at import time.[0m
[30;1m76 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m77 | [0m[35m`_version.py` also contains `$Revision$` markers, and the installation[0m
[30;1m78 | [0m[35mprocess marks `_version.py` to have this marker rewritten with a tag name[0m

[30;1m85 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m86 | [0m[35mPyGEOS functions support multithreading. More specifically, the Global[0m
[30;1m87 | [0m[35mInterpreter Lock (GIL) is released during function execution. Normally in Python, the[0m
[30;1m88 | [0m[35mGIL prevents multiple threads from computing at the same time. PyGEOS functions[0m
[30;1m89 | [0m[35minternally releases this constraint so that the heavy lifting done by GEOS can be[0m
[30;1m90 | [0m[35mdone in parallel, from a single Python process.[0m
[30;1m91 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m64 | [0m[35mPyGEOS functions support multithreading. More specifically, the Global[0m
[30;1m65 | [0m[35mInterpreter Lock (GIL) is released during function execution. Normally in Python, the[0m
[30;1m66 | [0m[35mGIL prevents multiple threads from computing at the same time. PyGEOS functions[0m
[30;1m67 | [0m[35minternally releases this constraint so that the heavy lifting done by GEOS can be[0m
[30;1m68 | [0m[35mdone in parallel, from a single Python process.[0m
